Local News

Decision on Industrial and Commercial Loan Association: Loans to be Implemented on August 1st; Organizational Charter, Detailed Rules of Procedure, and Detailed Loan Rules Revised and Promulgated by the Ministry of Finance Yesterday; Loan Association Convened Yesterday to Discuss Loan Disbursement Procedures 81

The Organizational Charter, Detailed Rules of Procedure, and Detailed Loan Rules of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee have been revised and approved by the Ministry of Finance and were instructed to be promulgated and implemented yesterday. The Loan Association convened its sixth meeting yesterday to discuss procedures for mortgage and credit loans, and decided to begin implementing loans on August 1st. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Meeting: After the Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee received instructions from the Ministry of Finance approving the various charters and rules, it convened its sixth committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday in the conference room on the second floor of the National Products Bank. Attendees included Cai Zengji, Du Yuesheng, Chen Guangfu, Song Ziliang, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Peishen, Wang Yansong, Yu Zuoting (represented by Wang Yansong), Bei Songsun (represented by Chen Guangfu), Xi Demao (represented by Zhang Peishen), Qin Runqing, and Wu Xingya (absent). Chairman Cai Zengji reported that the Organizational Charter, Detailed Rules of Procedure, and Detailed Loan Rules of the Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee had been revised and approved by the Ministry of Finance and were instructed to be promulgated. He expressed hope that the committee members would discuss and decide on issues such as the loan date and procedures in order to proceed. After the chairman's report, the committee members carefully read the various charters and rules approved by the Ministry of Finance, and then began discussions. It was resolved that (1) 15 million yuan would be used for mortgage loans to assist industry and commerce, and 5 million yuan would be used for credit loans, starting on August 1st; (2) the detailed loan rules, application forms, and investigation forms would be entrusted to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce for distribution. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 PM.

Application Procedures: According to Cai Zengji's statement to the Xin Xin News Agency reporter after yesterday's meeting, all the charters and rules for industrial and commercial loans have been approved by the Ministry of Finance. The meeting was held to decide on the loan date and procedures. It has now been decided to start loans on August 1st. The Organizational Charter, Detailed Loan Rules, application forms, and investigation forms have now been sent to print and will be delivered to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce within three days for distribution to member companies of various trade associations. Non-members of trade associations can directly collect them from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. Industrial and commercial companies should fill out the application form, together with the business license and balance sheet, profit and loss statement, etc., and submit them to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce for forwarding to the Loan Committee for review. Once approved, the loan will be disbursed.

Amount of Subscription: The Xin Xin News Agency reporter learned from banking circles yesterday that the total amount of industrial and commercial relief loans is 10 million yuan, of which 15 million yuan is for mortgage loans, which will be disbursed by various banks and money shops in accordance with the principles set by the Ministry. However, the application form and certificate must be reported to the committee for review. 5 million yuan is for credit loans, which will be managed by the Loan Association. The amount subscribed by the banking and money industries is now determined, with member banks of the Banking Association subscribing to 1 million yuan, the Money Industry Association subscribing to 250,000 yuan, and the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications subscribing to 2.5 million yuan, totaling 3.75 million yuan. The remaining shortfall will be covered by the banking and money industries continuing to solicit subscriptions from various banks and money shops in order to raise the full amount. All subscriptions separately determined by the banking and money industries will be deposited in the Chinese National Products Bank. Applicants for loans will be notified to apply for a loan from the bank after being reviewed and approved by the Loan Association. Both types of loans will be issued with national treasury certificates as a second guarantee in accordance with the loan amount.

Organizational Charter: The Organizational Charter of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee, Article 1: In order to assist industry and commerce in Shanghai, the Ministry of Finance has allocated 20 million yuan in national treasury certificates as a second guarantee for loans made by various banks and money shops in accordance with the ten loan principles promulgated by the Ministry. A committee is organized to handle review matters, named the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee (hereinafter referred to as the Committee). Article 2: The Committee has an unspecified number of members, appointed by the Minister of Finance. Article 3: The custody and receipt and issuance of national treasury certificates allocated by the Ministry of Finance shall be handled by the Chinese National Products Bank entrusted by the Committee. Article 4: The Committee shall have seven standing committee members to form a standing committee, and the standing committee members shall elect a chairman. Article 5: Meetings of the Committee and the Standing Committee shall be convened by the chairman. Article 6: When the Committee meets, if the chairman is unable to attend due to business, the standing committee members shall elect one person to serve as chairman. Article 7: When the Committee meets, each member must attend in person. If a member is unable to attend due to an accident, he/she may entrust another member of the Committee to attend on his/her behalf, but must declare it in writing in advance. Each member attending on behalf of another member is limited to representing one person. Article 8: Matters resolved by the Committee shall be implemented by the Standing Committee. Article 9: Important matters of the Committee shall be reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval at any time. Article 10: The Committee may borrow personnel from relevant banks and money shops to handle investigation and review matters. Article 11: The members and borrowed personnel of the Committee are all unpaid positions. Article 12: The Detailed Rules of Procedure and Detailed Loan Rules of the Committee shall be determined separately. Article 13: The Committee is temporarily located within the Chinese National Products Bank. Article 14: The Committee shall be dissolved upon completion of the loan review. All 20 million yuan in national treasury certificates used as the second guarantee for loans handled and issued by the Committee shall be handed over to the Ministry of Finance for verification and receipt by the various banks and money shops upon recovery of the loans. Article 15: Matters not covered in this Charter may be resolved by the Committee and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. Article 16: This Charter shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Finance.

Detailed Rules of Procedure: The Detailed Rules of Procedure of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee, Article 1: These Detailed Rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the Organizational Charter of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee. Article 2: Matters resolved by the Committee shall be implemented by the Standing Committee. External documents shall be signed by the chairman in the name of the Committee. Article 3: In the event of important matters that the Committee cannot decide, they shall be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for instructions. Article 4: In the event of urgent matters, the chairman may submit them to the Standing Committee for resolution, but must report to the Committee for ratification. Article 5: If the chairman is unable to attend a meeting due to business, the standing committee members shall elect one person to act on his/her behalf. Article 6: When the Committee receives mortgage loan certificates from various banks and money shops, the chairman shall submit them to the Committee for review and resolution by a majority of the members. Article 7: When the Committee receives applications for small credit loans and various documents from various factories and companies, it shall first send personnel to investigate, and then submit them for review. After completion, the chairman shall submit them to the Committee for review and resolution by a majority of the members. Article 8: For matters approved by the Committee, the chairman shall issue an approval document to notify the handling bank to fill out a national treasury certificate voucher for the loan bank to collect. For small credit loans, the handling bank shall be entrusted to disburse the loan. Article 9: When the bank or money shop recovers the loan, it shall immediately return the national treasury certificate voucher to the handling bank for counting. Article 10: If a staff member neglects his/her duties and causes damage to public funds, in addition to being liable for compensation, the chairman shall impose sanctions. If it involves dereliction of duty or fraud, it shall be dealt with strictly in accordance with the law. Article 11: Matters not covered in these Detailed Rules may be resolved by the Committee and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. Article 12: These Detailed Rules shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Finance.

Detailed Loan Rules: The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Rules, Article 1: The Ministry of Finance has allocated 20 million yuan in national treasury certificates as a second guarantee for loans to assist industry and commerce in Shanghai and has established the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee (hereinafter referred to as the Committee) to handle loan review matters. All procedures shall be handled in accordance with these Detailed Rules, unless otherwise stipulated by the laws and regulations promulgated by the Ministry. Article 2: Guaranteed loans are divided into the following two types: (1) Industrial and commercial mortgage loans, with a total amount limited to 15 million yuan, which shall be disbursed by banks and money shops themselves, but must be reported to the Committee for review; (2) Industrial and commercial small credit loans, with a total amount limited to 5 million yuan, which shall be disbursed by banks and money shops after depositing the separately determined funds in the Chinese National Products Bank and being reviewed and approved by the Committee. For both types of loans, national treasury certificates shall be issued in accordance with the loan amount as a second guarantee for the loan. Article 3: Mortgage loans are limited to factories that manufacture national products, businesses that sell national products, and those who transport national products for export. Article 4: National product factories or businesses that meet the following requirements may apply for loans: (1) For industrial and commercial mortgage loans, the value of the collateral is appropriate, the assets are solid, and it is certified by the lending bank or money shop; (2) For industrial and commercial small credit loans, two reputable businesses shall be jointly and severally responsible for guaranteeing repayment (if it is a limited company, the company's manager shall also be responsible for the guarantee). The assets of the borrower and guarantor are indeed solid and certified by the lending bank or money shop. Article 5: When factories or businesses apply for loan assistance, banks and money shops shall carefully verify the following: (1) Whether the factory or business is real; (2) The asset and liability situation; (3) The profit and loss situation; (4) Whether the business policy is sound; (5) Whether the purpose of the loan is necessary. Regarding the second and third items, if it is a company-organized factory or business, the most recent balance sheet and profit and loss statement shall be submitted together with the loan application to the bank or money shop for verification. However, this statement shall be limited to those certified by a well-known accountant or supervisor. Article 6: Lending banks and money shops may accept the following types of collateral, but only with the first mortgage right: (1) Goods; (2) Machinery and the factory building base; (3) Securities. Article 7: The collateral must meet the following conditions to be qualified: Goods: (1) Those that sell well in the market; (2) Those that are not easily perishable and have no risk of deformation or deterioration; (3) Those that are properly packaged; (4) Those that are stored in a solid warehouse; (5) Those with a stable market price; (6) Those insured by a reputable firm. Machinery: (1) New type and currently in use; (2) Those with higher manufacturing efficiency; (3) Those insured by a reputable firm. Factory building base: (1) Currently in operation, and the factory building is insured by a reputable firm. Securities: (1) Central and local government bonds that repay principal and interest on schedule; (2) Other reliable stocks and bonds with a market price. Article 8: The full amount of the mortgage loan shall be determined within the scope of the current market price or valuation (which shall be estimated by experts) of the collateral, but shall not exceed 70% of the current market price or valuation of the collateral. Article 9: When banks and money shops handle mortgage loans and borrowers request loan assistance, in addition to handling matters in accordance with the loan principles set by the Ministry, they shall fill out an application form and certificate and submit them to the Committee for review. The aforementioned application form shall state the name and address of the factory or business requesting the loan, the name of the manager, the type and value of the collateral, or the name and address of the guarantor, and its assets and liabilities, the amount of the loan, and the opinions of the lending bank or money shop. The format shall be determined separately. The aforementioned certificate shall be the sole responsibility of the various banks and money shops. Article 10: After the application form of the bank or money shop is reviewed and approved by the Committee and notified, the lending bank or money shop shall issue a receipt to the Committee to collect a national treasury certificate voucher equal to the full amount of the loan. Article 11: When factories and businesses request small credit loans, they shall submit an application form together with the business license and balance sheet, profit and loss statement, etc., to the Committee for review and loan disbursement. Article 12: If the collateral for mortgage loans is insufficient or inappropriate, or the guarantor business for small credit loans is unqualified, the Committee may reduce the loan amount or refuse to allocate national treasury certificates. Article 13: The loans stipulated in these Detailed Rules, regardless of whether there is collateral, shall be handled in accordance with the bill discounting loan method. However, the payment date of the bill issued by the borrower shall not exceed the deadline specified in the loan contract. Article 14: When banks and money shops discount bills issued by borrowers to colleagues, if there is collateral, it shall be collected by the lending bank or money shop. If there is no collateral, the bill issued by the borrower shall first be given to the guarantor business, and then the guarantor business shall be responsible for paying it to the lending bank or money shop, and no collateral custody certificate shall be required when rediscounting. The format of the aforementioned collateral custody certificate shall be determined separately. Article 15: Factories or businesses may repay the loan amount in one lump sum or in installments before the due date, with interest reduced as principal is reduced. The method shall be handled by the lending bank or money shop at its discretion. Article 16: If the loan applicant is already a guarantor business for a small credit loan, the loan standard amount shall include the amount guaranteed by the guarantor business (for example, if the applicant is qualified for a loan of 10,000 yuan, but has a guarantee responsibility of 3,000 yuan, then only 7,000 yuan can be loaned to him/her). Article 17: Matters not covered in these Detailed Rules may be resolved by the Committee and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. Article 18: These Detailed Rules shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Finance.

Founding of the Banking Association: Bank Acceptance Bills; Banking Associations Prepare to Organize Bill Acceptance Offices to Take Charge of Operations 82

Shen Shi News Agency reports that the Shanghai Banking Association, in order to alleviate the tight currency situation, has resolved to issue bank acceptance bills to circulate in the market. The small group committee has already decided that the reserve fund will be 30 million to 50 million yuan as a second collateral for acceptance bills. The Central Bank has also agreed to handle rediscounting. It is expected to be implemented in mid-August. A detailed report is as follows:

Creating Bank Acceptance Bills

Since the financial turmoil in Shanghai, a tight currency situation has resulted. Industry and commerce are suffering from the circulation of funds. The major banks in the city, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, etc., in view of this, have held meetings and discussions for days. As a result, they will recommend that the Banking Association create bank acceptance bills. After the last meeting of the Banking Association passed the principle and handed it over to the small group committee for handling, detailed methods have now been formulated. They will be implemented after being submitted to the Standing Committee and General Membership Meeting of the Banking Association for approval. Industry and commerce have also expressed their support for this method, so there is no problem with its realization.

Bank Acceptance Bills Have Double Guarantee

In order to handle bank acceptance bills, the Banking Association has decided to have the Bank Reserve Committee establish a bill acceptance office to be responsible for handling bank acceptance bill matters. Industrial and commercial customers with real goods can apply to the office for acceptance bills. After the office assesses the price, it will issue a bill with a corresponding amount of silver. Industrial and commercial customers can then take the bill to any member bank for discounting, which is extremely convenient. At the same time, in terms of credit, in addition to the specified goods as the first collateral in substance, there is also a reserve fund recognized by the joint reserve of the Banking Association as the second collateral, so its credit is more reliable than the promissory notes issued by individual banks. In the future, foreign trade can also handle trade finance, and its scope of circulation is extremely wide.

Increase Circulation by 50 Million

This time, the total amount of bank acceptance bills handled by the Banking Association is limited to about 30 million to 50 million yuan. The reserve fund part of the second guarantee will be subscribed by all 36 member banks separately. Negotiations are currently underway, so after the implementation of these acceptance bills, the financial sector can invisibly increase the circulation by 30 million to 50 million yuan. Not only will the funds of the industrial and commercial sectors be able to circulate as a result, but the Banking Association itself can also adjust through this bill.

Limit the Acceptance Quantity of Each Industry

These bank acceptance bills are currently being actively prepared by the joint reserve of the Banking Association and are expected to be realized in mid-August. The autumn agricultural products will be launched, and the demand for funds from the inland rural areas and the industrial and commercial sectors will be high, so it is necessary to realize them as soon as possible. According to reliable sources, there are strict allocation restrictions for each industry for these acceptance bills. The main ones are flour, cotton yarn, groceries, oils, cement, and national product factories producing quality export goods, etc., and corresponding quantities are limited according to the needs of each industry. The purpose of acceptance is to develop the national product production industry and support export purposes. The term of the acceptance bill shall not exceed four months at most.

Central Bank Agrees to Rediscount

In order to expand the scope of circulation, the Banking Association, which founded bank acceptance bills, needs to have the Central Bank handle rediscounting, so it has sent personnel for informal contact several times. Because it concerns financial relief, it has been approved to handle bank acceptance bill rediscounting and other businesses in accordance with the commercial acceptance bill method. Therefore, in the future, when various banks feel that they have absorbed an excessive amount of these bills, they can transfer them to the Central Bank for rediscounting in order to maintain stability.

Hurricane: To Land in Wenzhou; If Direction Does Not Change, Possible Impact on Shanghai; Rainy and Cloudy Yesterday, Hot, 91.9 Degrees 83

Guo Wen News Agency reports that a hurricane recently occurred in the South Pacific and has been blowing northward through Luzon and Taiwan for days. At 12:00 noon yesterday, the Shanghai Xujiahui Observatory received a report that the hurricane had reached 27 degrees north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude, and the direction was still west-northwest, which is close to Wenzhou and Fuzhou. If the direction does not change, it may impact Shanghai, but the coastal areas at the junction of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are obstructed by many mountains, and the wind may change direction after being obstructed. It is difficult to predict whether the direction will change. As for the wind force of the hurricane, it is said that it is about five to six in northeast Taiwan and the momentum is turning fierce in the eastern ocean, with a wind force of nine. However, the wind is in the ocean, which is different from the land. If the hurricane lands in Wenzhou, its momentum may be slightly reduced. There is another new hurricane rising in the Pacific Ocean, but it is far from Shanghai and the direction is unknown. The temperature yesterday was cool due to rainy and cloudy weather and a weak northeast wind, with a high of 91.9 degrees and a low of 77.5 degrees.

Another report states that since the beginning of summer, Shanghai has been dry with little rain, and it has almost caused a drought. Since the beginning of this month, there have been continuous rains, and in the last three days, there have been showers every day, so the fields have been sufficiently moistened. In addition, the rivers in the inner river ports are full of water, almost flush with the shore. If it rains again, it will damage agricultural affairs and harm cotton and rice. It is now feared that in lower fields, there is already too much water, and farmers are pumping water out. If the weather does not clear up and the rainfall increases by half a foot, it will inevitably lead to flooding.

The Yangtze River is a Vast Expanse: Jiangda Run Aground in Yangluo; China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Sends Steamer for Assistance 86

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River liner Jiangda, which departed from Shanghai for Hankou on the 17th of this month and arrived in Hankou on the 21st, was originally scheduled to return to Shanghai from Hankou today after loading and unloading goods and passengers. However, on the morning of the 21st, when the ship arrived at Yangluo, about 60 nautical miles from Hankou, the river water was extremely high, a vast expanse, and it was difficult to identify whether the track was a shallow shore or a deep place. The Jiangda sailed to the river surface opposite Yangluo, and the pilot accidentally drove onto a shoal, causing the ship to run aground and unable to move. It urgently telegraphed to the Shanghai and Hankou branches for help.

Telegram to Shanghai for Help: The place where the Jiangda ran aground is only a three-hour voyage from Hankou. Due to the flood, the waterway was mistaken, causing it to be deeply trapped. It has repeatedly reversed, but has failed to withdraw from the shoal. The Jianghua liner of the branch saw it and telegraphed to Shanghai for help through the captain of the Jianghua. The original telegram arrived at the branch yesterday afternoon, stating briefly that the Jiangda ran aground on the opposite bank of Yangluo. Due to the dangerous river water, it urgently needs to be towed and rescued. It is not advisable to delay the matter as the water recedes day by day. The Shanghai branch obtained the telegram and immediately telegraphed the Hankou branch to quickly dispatch the Liji liner to rush to tow and rescue.

Discharge Coal and Cargo: Now the most feared thing is that the draft of the hull will become shallower after the water recedes, making rescue difficult. Shipowner Feng Jun has now decided to discharge the cargo and coal in the Jiangda ship first to reduce the load. Then, when the Jiangda hull slightly rises above the water, it will carry out towing work. The shipping department of the branch has telegraphed the Hankou branch and instructed the Jiangda shipowner to do so.

"New Life Weekly" Case: Du Houyu's Appeal and Protest Argues That Article 367 of the Criminal Procedure Law Does Not Apply and Interprets the Meaning of Jurisdiction Defined by the Court Organization Law 89

According to New Sound News Agency, after the judgment in the New Life Weekly case, Hou Yu, the wife of Du Chongyuan, dissatisfied with the judgment of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, filed an independent appeal with the original trial court. However, this appeal was rejected by the Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court on the 20th of this month. It is learned that Mrs. Du also submitted a petition to the Supreme Court within the statutory period, requesting a redress of this case. Therefore, although the Second Branch of the High Court has rejected Mrs. Du's appeal, the hope for an appeal in this case has not yet been extinguished, and it is also heard that a protest has now been filed. The appeal and its written reasons are recorded below:

Criminal Appeal: In order to express disagreement with the fifth instance judgment made by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court regarding the case of my husband, Du Chongyuan, endangering foreign relations, declare appeal for cultural activities, respectfully requesting that the files be examined and handled. Upon investigation, my husband, Du Chongyuan, was sued for endangering foreign relations and sentenced by Jiangsu High Court Second Branch to one year and two months of imprisonment on July 9 of this year, and the judgment was concurrently made on July 11. Both the appellant and Du Chongyuan himself feel that this judgment cannot be accepted, and in accordance with Article 337 of the Criminal Procedure Law, for the benefit of the defendant, an independent appeal is filed against the first instance judgment. However, because the original trial court, after announcing the judgment, declared in court that this judgment could not be appealed and immediately ordered imprisonment to carry out the sentence, it clearly misunderstood the law. The reason for the misunderstanding is that it failed to study Article 368 of the Criminal Procedure Law in conjunction with Article 17, Paragraph 1 and Article 22, Paragraph 1 of the Court Organization Law, thereby confusing the first instance judgment of the High Court and its branch courts on the crime of endangering foreign relations with the second instance judgment, without distinguishing them. It also mistakenly believes that the applicable procedures specified in Article 367, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law are also provisions restricting appeals. It is not known whether an appeal should be allowed in this case is one issue, and whether the second or third instance procedure should be applied after the appeal is another issue. Article 367, Paragraph 2 of the Procedure Law only indicates that the Supreme Court's trial of appeals against first instance judgments of the High Court should apply the second instance procedure, and cannot restrict the application of Article 21, Paragraph 1 of the Court Organization Law. The original trial court's distortion is alarming. In order to prevent the original trial court from stubbornly adhering to its mistaken views, regarding the appellant's appeal, or from again misquoting Article 376 of the Criminal Procedure Law and rejecting it outright, in addition to separately filing an appeal with the original trial court, pointing out the errors, and separately submitting written reasons for the appeal in accordance with the statutory period, please forward them for review and judgment by the Supreme Court to redress the injustice. Respectfully submitted to the Supreme Court for review, by Hou Yu.

Reasons for Appeal: In order to supplement the reasons for the appeal in the case of Du Chongyuan's endangering foreign relations, against the first instance judgment made by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, my husband, Du Chongyuan, is the editor and publisher of "New Life Weekly". Because the 15th issue of Volume 2 of "New Life Weekly" on January 4 of this year contained an article entitled "Idle Talk of the Emperor" signed by Yi Shui, it was discovered by the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, who went to the Shanghai Municipal Government to request prosecution according to law. The Shanghai Municipal Police Department sent a letter to the prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court to initiate a public prosecution. The court ruled on July 9 of this year, "Du Chongyuan disseminated words to jointly defame, sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment, and confiscated the 15th issue of Volume 2 of 'New Life Weekly'," and instructed that this case belongs to the crime listed in Article 61 of the Criminal Law and, in accordance with Article 368 and Article 367, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, is not allowed to be appealed, and ordered to be sent to prison for execution on the same day. The appellant and Du Chongyuan himself firmly disagree with the above judgment, and believe that the distortion of the ruling is suspected of deliberately destroying the law. In accordance with the provisions of Article 327 of the Criminal Procedure Law, within the statutory appeal period, errors were made and appeal documents were submitted to the original trial court and the appellate court on the same day, declaring disagreement for the benefit of the defendant. Now, in accordance with the period stipulated in Article 374 of the Criminal Procedure Law, I am submitting additional reasons, which are detailed as follows: (1) Whether the appeal should be allowed, (2) Whether the conditions for prosecution are met, and (3) Whether there is criminal responsibility. (1) Whether the appeal should be allowed. Upon investigation, the original trial court recognized that the defendant Du Chongyuan had committed the crime of harming the reputation of the head of a friendly country and made a judgment of sentencing. This is the first instance criminal judgment for endangering foreign relations listed in Article 17, Paragraph 1 of the Court Organization Law. This first instance judgment can be appealed and should be under the jurisdiction of the Supreme Court, as clearly stated in Article 22, Paragraph 1 of the Court Organization Law. Although the statutory principal penalty for the crime of defamation is listed in Article 61 of the Criminal Law and should be subject to the restriction of Article 368 of the Criminal Procedure Law, which does not allow appeals to the third instance, defamation of the head of a friendly country is an independent crime under Article 116 of the Criminal Law. Since the new Criminal Procedure Law does not have an equivalent provision to Article 12 of the old Criminal Procedure Law, it cannot be equated with cases that should be subject to Article 368 of the Criminal Procedure Law, which does not allow appeals to the third instance, simply because the principal penalty for ordinary defamation is within the scope listed in Article 61 of the Criminal Law. Moreover, the so-called cases that cannot be appealed to the third instance court in that article are clearly limited to cases that have already been judged by the second instance. According to Article 17, Paragraph 1 of the Court Organization Law and Article 4 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the original trial jurisdiction is clearly the first instance and not the second instance. How can its first instance judgment claim to be the second instance and say that it should be subject to the restriction of not allowing appeals? Or it is said that the original trial court's distortion of the law is that it confuses the provision in Article 367, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, which states that "appeals against first instance judgments of the High Court also apply the third instance procedure," with the provision in Article 368 of the same law, and mistakenly believes that they both belong to the legal provisions restricting appeals to the third instance court. It should be known that the main purpose of Article 367, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law is to stipulate the procedure that should be applied when the highest court hears appeals against first instance judgments of the High Court, that is, its appeal must be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 369 and subsequent articles of the same law, and not according to the second instance trial procedure. It has nothing to do with the question of whether the first instance judgment made by the High Court should be allowed to be appealed. If it were not for taking the text out of context and omitting the words "trial by the highest court," there would be no possibility of distortion. The wording of Article 368 of the same law also states that cases that have been judged by the second instance cannot be appealed to the third instance court, and does not state that cases judged by the High Court cannot be appealed to the highest court. Its original legislative intention is very clear. From the perspective of legislative reasons, the first instance jurisdiction court for cases of endangering foreign relations is the High Court, which is intended to show special caution because these cases are related to national security. How can there be any intention to suppress appeals? If a guilty verdict is received by the defendant, what would be the repercussions when a miscarriage of justice occurs? If a verdict of not guilty is received by the defendant, what happens upon their exoneration? Modern countries with a legal system absolutely do not adopt the principle of single-level trial in ordinary litigation. There are only slight differences in the number of trials. The Criminal Procedure Law clearly states the principle of three trials and lists several cases of minor crimes, which, after being judged by the second instance, cannot be appealed to the third instance as an exception. Since endangering foreign relations must not be regarded as a minor crime and relates to national security, and its first instance is under special jurisdiction, those who should be civil and administrative judges have created a strange theory of one instance finality, not allowing appeals. This is known to those who know the law to be absurd. Although this does not involve the main issue of the original judgment being illegal, it is related to whether this appeal is legal. Therefore, it is specially explained in advance in order to correct the illegal matters instructed by the original trial during the pronouncement. (2) Whether the conditions for prosecution are met. Article 119 of the Criminal Law stipulates that the crime of defamation in Article 116 and the crime in Article 118 must be prosecuted upon the request of the foreign government. The manner of the request is also clearly stipulated in Article 220, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law. The Judicial Yuan's Interpretation No. 753 on June 7, 1932 also clearly states that this term must be a legal term of the foreign government or someone who can represent the foreign government. Based on the above legal articles and interpretations, it is clear that the crime of defamation in Article 116 of the Criminal Law must be legally stated by the foreign government or someone who can represent the foreign government in order to meet the conditions for prosecution. Now, upon investigation of the facts stated in the original judgment and the original indictment, this case was only requested by the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai to the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Municipal Government ordered the Public Security Bureau to forward it for investigation and prosecution. The Consul-General in Shanghai cannot be regarded as the representative of the foreign government, and there is the aforementioned interpretation for reference, which is beyond doubt. The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Public Security Bureau cannot regard themselves as the highest officials of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Judicial Administration. Therefore, both the requester and the recipient of the request are not qualified, which means that the request cannot be regarded as legal. There are still shortcomings in the essential elements of the prosecution. The prosecutor's hasty public prosecution and the original trial's judgment on the substantive criminal law are both cases of acceptance without being accepted and violate the law. Responsibility lies with all, and in accordance with the provisions of Article 375, Paragraph 5 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the original trial should naturally be deemed inappropriate, and there is no room for applying Article 372 of the same law. (3) Whether there is criminal responsibility. Article 12 of the Criminal Law stipulates that conduct is not punishable if it is not intentional or negligent, that is, anything that is not intentional cannot be called the person's conduct, that is, it cannot be said that the person has committed a crime. The punishment for negligent conduct is limited to those that are specifically stipulated in the special provisions of the Criminal Law. According to the principle of criminal responsibility stipulated in this Criminal Law, the crime of defamation by disseminating words in Article 310 of the Criminal Law, in addition to those who commit the criminal act and those who knowingly assist, there is no so-called person who is naturally responsible in law. Because the Criminal Law and the Publication Law, which is a special law, are clearly different, the penalties in the Publication Law clearly stipulate which ones should make the publisher, editor, author, and printer jointly responsible, and which ones should make only one of them solely responsible. The crime of defamation by disseminating words in the Criminal Law only requires those who commit the crime and those who knowingly assist to be responsible. If the publisher and editor can prove that they did not know and participate, there is no basis for making them jointly responsible. The 15th issue of Volume 2 of "New Life Weekly" was published on May 4 of this year, and Du Chongyuan stayed in Jiangxi before that issue. The letter from the Jiangxi Pottery Administration has been submitted, which proves that Du Chongyuan did not participate in the publication and distribution of "Idle Talk of the Emperor" and did not know about it. Even if he should be blamed for dereliction of duty because he held the title of publisher and editor, or because he entrusted someone to edit on his behalf and entrusted the wrong person, there is no provision for punishing negligence in the crime of defamation under the law. The original trial was unwilling to conduct detailed trials and research on whether the article was a foreign submission, whether the author Yi Shui had another person, and whether the manuscripts for that issue had actually been selected by Du Chongyuan. They only believed that because Du Chongyuan held the position of editor and publisher, he should naturally be responsible in law. It is difficult to say that he has done his best in the trial. (Omission) Therefore, in addition to the improper distinction of criminal responsibility, the original judgment cannot be said to be erroneous in the application of criminal provisions. For the above reasons, I should ask the Supreme Court to review and, in accordance with the provisions of Article 271, Paragraph 5, Article 389, Article 390, Paragraph 2, and Article 295, Paragraph 1, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Procedure Law, revoke the original judgment and instruct that this case should not be accepted, or immediately make a judgment of not guilty for the defendant Du Chongyuan. Respectfully submitted to the Supreme Court for review. (To be continued)

The Southeast China Branches United General Office of the World Red Swastika Society received a telegram yesterday from the General Office and the Jiujiang Branch, reporting on the flood relief measures. Jiaxiang, Yuncheng, Juye and other counties have been graded into teams by the Jining branch, carrying Wonder Bread, baked cakes and medicines to provide emergency relief. As for the disaster situation in Henan Province, Yanshi is the most severely affected, with the entire county submerged. A telegram has been sent to transfer funds to the Zhengzhou Red Swastika Society to handle emergency relief nearby. We appeal to the united branches to raise funds together to save the disaster-stricken people. Also received a telegram from the Jiujiang Red Swastika Society that Tianmen and Gucheng in Hubei Province have been submerged, and more than 100,000 disaster victims have drowned. A urgent telegram was sent earlier requesting the dispatch of a team to retrieve and bury the bodies along the river. At present, corpses are being retrieved here every day, with more than 800 bodies having been retrieved. Floating corpses are washed away by large islands, and most of the limbs are incomplete. There is a family, large and small, who have all died, and are still holding on tightly without letting go. Also received telegrams from the Beijing, Wuhu, and Tongqing Red Swastika Societies that they have dispatched teams and multiple ships to cruise along the Yangtze River to retrieve the floating bodies in Tianmen, Gucheng, and other counties.

Third Instance Litigation Costs Remitted Directly to the Supreme Court 96

The Ministry of Judicial Administration recently issued a document unifying the method of paying third instance litigation costs and notified the First and Second Special Zones and the Shanghai Local Court in this port, stating: "In cases where a Supreme Court appeal is encountered and the third instance fee has not been paid, the original court should, in accordance with the provisions of Article 478 and Article 439, Paragraph 2 of the Civil Procedure Law, order the parties to remit the fee directly to the Accounting Section of the Supreme Court within the correction period, issue a receipt, and the parties should submit the receipt to the original court for verification. If the parties still pay to the original court, there is no need to pay on their behalf. Please investigate and handle accordingly." Luo, the president of the Shanghai Local Court, has already instructed the clerks at the reception office to comply with this order.

Shop Owner's Concubine Steals Stamp and Check to Defraud Funds; Manager Discovers, Reports to Police, and Arrest is Made 99

Chen Chixin Machinery Shop, located at 427 Tiantong Road, is an investment by Ningbo native Chen Baoquan (aka Ah Jin) and others. Chen has a concubine named Qian Ayue, who is 29 years old. She lives in the shop. However, Qian is addicted to gambling, resulting in heavy debt. On the 16th of this month, Chen Baoquan went to Ningbo on business. Fearing the shop would need funds, he gave a checkbook from Dunxu Bank and two stamps to the manager, Zhang Liaoming. Unexpectedly, the day before yesterday, Zhang suddenly discovered that the checkbook and stamps were missing. He went to Dunxu Bank to inquire and was told that on the 20th, a woman had presented a 300-yuan check for withdrawal. The bank had verified that the signature matched Chen Baoquan's and had paid the money. Zhang suspected Qian and reported it to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. Detective Ye Yusi was dispatched to arrest Qian. A key that matched the one on the counter and silver dollars worth 26 yuan were found during a search and taken back to the police station. Qian confessed without hesitation. Besides the 26 yuan recovered, the rest of the money had already been used to pay off gambling debts. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Fifth Tribunal of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Li Zhishan, explained the situation and charged her with stealing and misusing stamps under articles 217 section 2 and 322 of the criminal law, requesting severe punishment. Zhang Ziming stated in court that the check, etc., were locked in a drawer at the time. He hired a lawyer to file a civil suit, requesting that the criminal judgment include a simultaneous ruling. When questioned, the defendant Qian Ayue confessed. Judge Dai Rongduo, after reviewing the confession, postponed the hearing because the case required further investigation.

No Wrongdoing in Qianzhuang's Stock Withdrawal; Wu Jincheng Not Guilty 100

After the collapse of the Yikang Fengji Qianzhuang (money shop), Yao Yaoming, owner of Youcheng Lumber Company, who had a large sum deposited in the shop, filed a lawsuit against the shop owner, Wu Jincheng, seeking compensation. Bao Xianfa and Others Sentenced for Forging Divorce Document 101

Bao Xianfa, a senior staff member in the export department of Xiangmao Foreign Company, had a relationship with the widow Shen Shanwen (aka Shen Sikuan). The relationship deteriorated, and Shen accused Bao of abandonment in the First Special Court. During the trial, Bao presented a document of separation, claiming he had divorced Shen. The document was witnessed by Xu Jinfang, who said that 250 yuan had been delivered to Shen through Zhang Lianbao. As a result, Bao was acquitted. Shen, however, accused Bao, Xu, and Zhang of forging the document in the First Special Court. After several interrogations by the court, the document was authenticated twice. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Zhaoxin of the Eighth Tribunal announced the verdict: Bao Xianfa and Zhang Lianbao were each sentenced to two months imprisonment for jointly forging a private document sufficient to harm others. Xu Jinfang was sentenced to three months imprisonment for jointly forging a private document sufficient to harm others. The forged separation document was confiscated.

Shanghai Aviation Association Headquarters Holds 21st Meeting; Shanghai Municipal Government Approves Donation Method for Sand and Stone Industry 102

Yuxing Steamer Runs Aground in Quanzhou; Details Await Captain's Report 103

The Yuxing steamer, owned by Zhaoxing Company, originally sailed on the Russian Far East route. Recently, the steamer was chartered to transport goods from Yingkou to Fujian and Quanzhou. It was fully loaded with soybean cakes, grains, etc., from Niuzhuang to Xingquan for unloading and then transport goods from that port to Shanghai. On the morning of the 21st of this month, the steamer safely arrived in Quanzhou. While entering the port of Quanzhou, the steamer accidentally strayed from the waterway and ran aground on a reef.

After running aground, it withdrew. The waters near Xiaozhui Island in the port of Quanzhou have many reefs, making navigation difficult. Because of the careless route taken by the Yuxing, it hit a reef near Xiaozhui Island. The ship was suddenly stranded on the reef and could not move. The captain immediately engaged reverse thrust to move the ship off the reef. After some time, it was finally able to reach the port of Quanzhou.

Report to Shanghai. Yesterday, Zhaoxing Company received a telegram from the captain of the Yuxing, stating that the steamer ran aground near Xiaozhui Island when entering the port of Quanzhou at 10:30 a.m. on the 21st. The ship anchored in the port at 11:30 a.m. and was not taking on water. The telegram did not provide details on whether the hull was damaged. Further details will be available once the captain provides a detailed report. Yesterday, the company sent a letter to the China Ship Insurance Joint Association for investigation.

Shanghai's Anti-Smoking Campaign is in Full Swing; Municipal Government Issues Notice for Registration of Smokers; The Poor are Sent to Anti-Smoking Hospitals for Free Treatment 106

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, under the order of the Municipal Government, is in charge of the registration of smokers in Shanghai. Yesterday morning, it issued a notice that from today until the end of September is the deadline for smokers to report their addiction. All smokers in Shanghai should register with the bureau as scheduled. Those who voluntarily want to quit smoking but are too poor to afford medical treatment will be sent to anti-smoking hospitals for free treatment within these three months. Those who cannot quit immediately due to illness will be issued a limited-time smoking permit, allowing them to purchase and smoke opium paste. If they do not voluntarily register before September of this year, the period from October to the end of December will be the compulsory registration period. The bureau will fine captured smokers while forcing them to register. The bureau's regulations for smoker registration have also been officially announced. Details are as follows:

Municipal Public Security Bureau Notice Regarding Registration. Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Notice Fa Zi No. 137. It is well known that opium is extremely harmful and has long been banned. However, Shanghai is a city where people from all over gather, both good and bad are mixed, and unscrupulous people secretly open dens for people to smoke. Citizens indulge in their habits and do not pull themselves together. Therefore, although strict bans have been enforced, opium has not been eradicated. The reason for this is that Shanghai's anti-smoking program has not been publicized, treatment for smokers has not been widespread, and the management of opium sales has not been carried out according to regulations. Since April of this year, when the bureau received the "Implementation Measures for Banning Opium," we have drafted anti-smoking plans and requested instructions. Recently, the Municipal Government issued the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period," ordering us to conduct smoker registration from this month until the end of December this year, etc. We have also drafted "Detailed Rules for Implementing Smoker Registration" and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation. From today until the end of September is the deadline for smokers to voluntarily report. All smokers in Shanghai should register with the bureau as scheduled. Those who voluntarily want to quit smoking but are too poor to afford medical treatment will be sent to anti-smoking hospitals for free treatment within these three months. Those who cannot quit immediately due to illness will be issued a limited-time smoking permit, allowing them to purchase and smoke opium paste. The bureau has printed "Smoker Registration Application Forms" and "Smoker Registration Instructions" and distributed them to all bureaus, police stations, and sub-stations and outposts, so that smokers can obtain them anywhere, advise each other, and register with the bureau. If they do not voluntarily register before September of this year, the period from October to the end of December will be the compulsory registration period. The bureau will strictly investigate and punish all captured opium smokers with a fine of 50 yuan to 300 yuan according to regulations, and force them to register. After the registration deadline at the end of December, the bureau will stop issuing smoking permits. All smokers caught thereafter will be fined according to the promulgated regulations and sent to anti-smoking hospitals for compulsory treatment. It should be known that the bureau is carrying out this anti-smoking campaign in strict accordance with the high command's strict order to eradicate opium, with the determination to thoroughly eliminate it. During the registration period, we will first persuade, then force, and promote the campaign step by step. We urge all smokers in Shanghai to carefully examine and register, ensuring that no one is missed, so that after the registration deadline this year, we will have accurate data on the number of smokers and the amount and quality of opium consumed, and then gradually reduce it year by year, so that there is a standard. Five days after the posting of this notice, if there is any secret operation of trafficking or opening of opium dens for people to smoke, once discovered, the offenders will be handed over to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for handling according to military law in accordance with the anti-smoking regulations issued by the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and their property will be confiscated. This notice is hereby issued for general information. Everyone must abide by it and not violate it. Be sure.

Promulgated Smoker Registration Instructions. (1) The Significance of Smoker Registration. The purpose of the smoker registration carried out by the bureau is to ascertain the precise number of smokers in Shanghai, in order to have a standard for gradually reducing smoking year by year, so that all smokers can quit completely within a specified period. (2) Registration Deadline. The registration period for smokers in Shanghai is set at six months, divided into two phases. The first phase, from July to the end of September this year, is the voluntary registration period for smokers. All smokers in Shanghai must register with the bureau voluntarily. The second phase, from October to the end of December this year, is the compulsory registration period. The bureau will summon and question captured smokers. (3) Matters for Smoker Registration. Smokers who voluntarily report or are forcibly registered, those who voluntarily want to quit smoking will be sent to the hospital for treatment, and those who cannot quit immediately due to illness will be issued a smoking permit, allowing them to purchase and smoke opium paste temporarily, and gradually reduce the amount smoked. (4) Registration Application Form. (1) Smokers should first fill out a registration application form in order to obtain a limited-time smoking permit or await referral to an anti-smoking hospital. (2) The bureau has prepared three types of registration application forms: one for applying for an ordinary limited-time smoking permit, one for applying for a limited-time smoking permit for the poor, and one for requesting to quit smoking. The aforementioned application forms have been printed and distributed to all sub-bureaus, police stations, and sub-stations and outposts for smokers to obtain anywhere. (5) Obtaining an Ordinary Limited-Time Smoking Permit. (1) Applicants for an ordinary limited-time smoking permit should personally submit the registration application to the bureau for registration. The registration application form can be filled out in advance or temporarily at the bureau. Immediately pay the permit fee and obtain the limited-time smoking permit. (2) If the applicant is unable to personally submit the application to the bureau due to illness, they can fill out a registration application form, along with the permit fee, and ask someone to obtain the permit at the bureau. (3) The applicant can submit the registration application form and permit fee to the household registration office of the sub-bureau or police station in charge, immediately obtain a receipt, and go to the original agency where the registration application form was submitted three days later to exchange it for a limited-time smoking permit. (6) Obtaining a Limited-Time Smoking Permit for the Poor. (1) Applicants for a limited-time smoking permit for the poor should fill out a registration application form and a guarantee form, along with the permit fee, and submit them to the bureau or its subordinate sub-bureaus and police stations, immediately obtain a receipt, and come to the bureau or go to the original agency where the registration application form was submitted one week later to exchange it for a limited-time smoking permit for the poor. (2) Qualifications of the Guarantor. Any friend or relative of the smoker with a confirmed address and family can be a guarantor. (3) If the bureau determines that an applicant for a limited-time smoking permit for the poor is not actually poor, they should be punished in accordance with the provisions of items B and C of Article 5 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period." The original text is recorded below: Item B of Article 5 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period": "Those who are not truly poor shall not fraudulently obtain this type of permit for the poor. Violators shall not only be required to obtain an ordinary limited-time smoking permit but shall also be fined three to five times the permit fee of five yuan stipulated in Article 9 of the Regulations for Suppressing Smokers." Item C: "The permit for the poor must be issued only after the local Baozhang or Jiazhang has filled out a certificate proving that it is true. If there is any false reporting or concealment, the person providing the certificate shall be fined half the amount of the fine imposed." (4) Smokers who are illiterate can invite a guarantor to go to the bureau or its affiliated agencies to apply for registration. All registration application forms, guarantees, etc., can be filled out by the bureau staff and the household registration or internal affairs police officers of each sub-bureau and police station. (7) Limited-Time Smoking Permit for Travelers. When smokers travel to various places, they should submit the limited-time smoking permit they have obtained to the bureau, immediately pay the fee, and apply to exchange it for a limited-time smoking permit for travelers. (8) Fee Amount and Validity Period. The fee for each ordinary limited-time smoking permit is five yuan. The fee for each limited-time smoking permit for the poor is six jiao. The fee for each limited-time smoking permit for travelers is three yuan. Limited-time smoking permits must be exchanged every six months. The validity period of a travel permit is three months. (9) Requesting to Quit Smoking. (1) Smokers who request to quit smoking during voluntary registration will be sent to the municipal anti-smoking hospital for free treatment to show special consideration. (2) Smokers who request to quit smoking should fill out a request to quit smoking application form and submit it in person to the bureau or its subordinate agencies for investigation and registration. The registration application form can also be filled out temporarily upon submission. Immediately obtain a receipt and await the scheduled referral to the anti-smoking hospital. (3) The request to quit smoking application form should list the name and address of the guarantor, and the guarantor should sign and affix their seal. If the smoker deliberately evades and does not report to the bureau when the time for referral comes, the guarantor will be responsible for investigating and summoning them, and their registration qualification will be revoked. (10) Penalties for Failure to Register During the Compulsory Registration Period. They will be ordered to register retroactively, and people will be allowed to report them. If the report is verified, a percentage of the fine will be awarded as a reward. The methods for punishment and rewarding people for reporting will be implemented in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period." The original text is recorded below: Article 4 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period": "During the compulsory registration period, those who still conceal and attempt to evade registration will be allowed to be reported secretly by the people. Once verified, in addition to being registered retroactively in accordance with regulations, they will also be fined 50 yuan to 300 yuan. Those who make false accusations will be punished in reverse in accordance with the law. Thirty percent of the aforementioned fine will be awarded to the informant." (11) Handling After the End of the Compulsory Registration Period. After the end of the compulsory registration period, limited-time smoking permits will no longer be issued. If there are still people who secretly smoke and have not registered, after being discovered by the bureau, they will be punished in accordance with regulations and forced to quit. (12) The Basis for the Bureau's Suppression of Opium Smokers Thereafter. 1. After the registration of smokers in Shanghai, all suspects arrested for smoking opium will first be sent to an anti-smoking hospital for testing. If the test confirms that they are not addicted to opium, they will be released immediately. 2. After the registration of smokers in Shanghai, all cases of opening dens for people to smoke and other major trafficking cases discovered by the bureau will be handled in accordance with Article 8 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period" issued by the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and Articles 3 and 20 of the "Regulations for Strictly Prohibiting Narcotics and Suppressing Opium Paste Shops." The original text is recorded below: Article 8 of the "Measures for Registering Smokers During the Registration Period": "Limited-time smoking permits are absolutely not allowed to be used to open dens for people to smoke. Violators will have their property confiscated and will be severely punished in accordance with military law." Article 3 of the "Regulations for Strictly Prohibiting Narcotics and Suppressing Opium Paste Shops": "Those who smuggle opium and other supplies shall be subject to strict inspection by specially established anti-smuggling agencies or local governments at important semi-finished product routes, railway stations, ports, post office parcel bureaus, airports, and during travel. Once discovered, the smuggled goods shall be confiscated and destroyed, and the offenders shall be severely punished in accordance with military law. Their private property shall be confiscated after verification and handed over to the informant and the personnel in charge of the case in accordance with regulations." Article 20 of the "Regulations for Strictly Prohibiting Narcotics and Suppressing Opium Paste Shops": "Those who operate without the approval of the competent authority and the issuance of a special license shall be deemed to be engaged in smuggling, regardless of whether the opium paste sold is affixed with stamps. Once discovered, the offenders shall be punished in accordance with military law, and their private goods and property shall be confiscated after verification and handed over to the informant and the personnel in charge of the case." (13) Matters Requiring Attention by Smokers. After the registration of smokers in Shanghai, if the sub-bureaus and police teams deliberately create difficulties in handling smoker registration, if the arrested opium smokers are detained without cause or punished privately, or if the investigators and police officers dispatched by the bureau engage in malfeasance and solicit money, the people are allowed to send letters or come to the bureau to report them, and we will send personnel to investigate and handle them severely in accordance with the law. However, if the accusations are false, they will also be punished in reverse in accordance with the law.

Shanghai Municipal Council Decides to Postpone Tax Increase for Rickshaws; Business Vehicles Limited to Current Number; Vehicles Detained Released and July Licenses Issued Upon Payment 107

According to the New Voice News Agency, the rickshaw and handcart industries opposed the Shanghai Municipal Council's increase in taxes and petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Council Taxpayers' Association in the afternoon. The Shanghai Municipal Council committee held a meeting on Friday and decided to postpone the tax increase for the two industries. Public Safety Bureau and Public Works Bureau Launch "Clean the Walls" Campaign; Orders Sent to Each Police Station for Implementation; Regarding Notices and Posters for Renting 108

The Director of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau, Cai Jinjun, in order to promote the New Life Movement, jointly with the Public Works Bureau, launched a "Clean the Walls" campaign. Yesterday, specific orders were issued to each branch bureau and police station, requiring all property owners to install signs specifically for tenants to post rental notices, in order to beautify the city's appearance. It is understood that regarding the promotion of the New Life Movement and the arrangement of notices and slogans in this city, this Bureau has already dispatched personnel to jointly discuss with the Public Works Bureau the "Clean the Walls" campaign, and the measures have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. At each alley entrance, this Bureau's respective jurisdictional offices should require property owners to install signs specifically for tenants to post notices. Hereafter, if tenants still disorderly post notices at alley entrances, they should be punished according to Article 13 of the Municipal Notice Management Regulations. It is now determined that the notice boards at each alley entrance must be uniformly erected by the property owners within half a month under the order of the heads of each branch bureau and station. Hereafter, all rental advertisements at each alley entrance should be posted within the designated boards and must not be disorderly. Violators will be punished according to Article 23 of the Advertising Regulations. These notices will serve as a warning and improve the city's appearance. In addition to the separate orders, a copy of Article 13 of the Advertising Regulations is extracted below. This order states that those who post advertisements at the following locations without the permission of the Public Works Bureau will be fined up to ten silver dollars: (1) Bulletin boards of party and government agencies; (2) Outer walls of government offices, schools, and other public buildings; (3) Gates; (4) Utility poles; (5) Sides of trams, buses, and long-distance buses; (6) Walls along "Clean Walls" routes; (7) Walls where government offices or property owners have posted prohibitions against posting.

After the Collapse of Minghua Bank, the Shanghai Branch Cannot Be Sorted Out; Responsible Persons Are Not in Shanghai; Creditors File Lawsuit with the Court 109

The Minghua Bank on Henan Road, after the collapse of its Qingdao headquarters, took the same action and declared its closure, which has been over a month. It has no way to deal with the various debts it owes. The chairman of the bank, Tong Jinhui, is reportedly being detained by the Qingdao authorities, and the assistant manager, Miao Zhendong, is also in Qingdao, being monitored by local creditors in a hotel, fearing his escape. The general manager, Zhang Jiongbo, from Ningbo, is rumored to have returned to his hometown to evade debts, but others say he is still in Qingdao. Therefore, only the deputy manager, Yu Dehua, remains in Shanghai, making it increasingly difficult to quickly conduct the Shanghai branch's liquidation affairs. In general, depositors, because there is no prospect of repayment, have recently filed criminal lawsuits against the responsible persons of the bank with the First Special District Local Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Zhaoxin opened a court session to examine the case of fraud and breach of trust brought by Qian Zhen against Tong, Zhang, Yu, and Miao. Of the four defendants, only Yu Dehua, accompanied by his defense lawyer, appeared in court. Qian Zhen stated in his complaint that he was originally from Zhenhai and worked in Shanghai. On May 1st of last year, he deposited 300 yuan, his savings, in the bank for a one-year term, and this year he continued to deposit for another year. Unexpectedly, it suddenly closed down in less than three weeks. This situation is a breach of faith and a fraud against depositors. Judge Yang then stated that since many of the defendants in this case had not appeared in court, and there were multiple lawsuits filed against the bank, he had already sent a letter to the Qingdao authorities to inquire about the progress of the liquidation. He stated that the case could only be clarified after receiving a reply from Qingdao, and adjourned the hearing to the afternoon of July 31st.

Notorious Bandit Leader from Jiangbei, Yue Youwei, Arrested; Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters Requests Transfer 111

Yue Youwei, a notorious bandit leader from Jiangbei, also known as Feng Youcai, nicknamed "Marshal Yue," and also known as "Baldy Yue" because of his pockmarked head, is 44 years old and from Funing. He has over three to four thousand followers and possesses all kinds of firearms. He has committed numerous cases of kidnapping, extortion, arson, murder, and robbery in the counties of Xu, Huai, and Hai in Jiangbei. Recently, he fled to Shanghai to hide. The county governments of Yancheng and thirteen other counties reported this to their superiors, who approved a bounty for his arrest. The Zhenjiang Garrison Commander, Xiang Zhizhuang, secretly ordered the deputy director of the special affairs team, Hu Zhen, to bring his detectives to Shanghai to secretly investigate with the Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau. Until the 21st, Hu Zhen received a tip from an informant that Yue was hiding in Room 31, Wuling Apartment, No. 2 Lane, 244 Baille Road, in the French Concession. Hu immediately, together with detectives from the Municipal Public Safety Bureau, Wang Zhengrong, etc., reported to the French Concession police station at 1:45 a.m. yesterday and dispatched Western detectives led by Deputy Inspector Lu Zhixiang and Detective Song Yunfeng, etc., to the address of Room 31 in Wuling Apartment. They found Yue and his follower, Fei Jinhong (40 years old, from Funing), inside the room and immediately arrested them both, taking them back to the police station for detention. Yesterday at noon, they were sent to the First Criminal Division of the Special Second Court, where Judge Wang Gangxu, along with clerk Zheng Rongsheng, interrogated them. First, they asked the defendants Yue and Fei about their ages and origins. According to Yue, he came to Shanghai to look for work but has not found it yet. Fei stated that his wife used to run a cloth factory business, but it stopped after her death and he is currently unemployed. Then, the Bureau of Police's lawyer, Fei Xizhen, presented the case, stating briefly that the defendants were notorious bandit leaders from Jiangbei and that the police station had received a request for assistance from the Zhenjiang Garrison Command to arrest them. The Garrison Command had no objection to the transfer. Hu Lingxing and Wang Zhengrong, who came from the Command, also submitted a statement detailing the process of arresting the defendants. They also stated that the Command had prepared a document to the Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau requesting permission to transfer the defendants for investigation. The court verified the statements and, since the request for transfer from the Command did not have a valid official document and the procedures were incomplete, ordered that they would be handled after receiving a letter from the Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau. The defendants were detained.

Brawl over Buying Shaved Ice; Result of the Autopsy on the Murder Case: Xu Heshang Died from Injuries; Suspect Lu Axiao Should Be Prosecuted 115

Xu Heshang, a local resident residing at No. 8, Lane 310, Tangshan Road, 44 years old, bought shaved ice from Lu Axiao (from Nanxiang, 22 years old), who set up a cold drink stall in front of the Fuxingguan Congee Shop at No. 643, Dongyouheng Road, at around 8 a.m. on the 17th of this month. He did not pay the copper coins, leading to a dispute between the two, which then turned into a mutual brawl. Afterwards, Xu returned home and felt chest pain after being beaten. He died suddenly at around 1 p.m. the next day. Xu's wife, Zhang, then went to Lu's place and reported him, and he was detained in the Jiaxing Road Police Station. Hua Detective Jin Yangwu and others were dispatched to investigate, and Xu's body was taken to the autopsy site on Feilun Road. The next morning, Lu was sent to the First Special Court for detention. The procuratorate of the court commissioned prosecutors to go to the autopsy site to examine the body. At the time, the cause of death could not be determined from the external appearance of the body, so it was decided to perform an autopsy to clarify the truth. This has already been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, the autopsy was completed, and it was found that two of the deceased's left ribs were broken and he had symptoms of tuberculosis. At around 10 a.m., Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuyi, etc., were commissioned by the Special First Court to go to the site and inform the relevant police station of the autopsy results. They questioned the defendants briefly. Guo then concluded that the deceased Xu Heshang, male, did die from injuries sustained during his life. The suspect Lu Axiao should be prosecuted by the police station and sent to the court for handling. The body was handed over to his wife, Xu Zhang, for burial after she signed a bond.

Liquidators of Huaying Pharmacy Request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Try Mediation; The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Has Agreed to Accept 117

After Huaying Pharmacy closed down, the shareholders' meeting entrusted lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Yuan Xingyun, and accountant Qin Kai, to handle the liquidation. It is heard that the liquidators have now prepared a mediation plan and sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to try mediation in accordance with the new bankruptcy law's mediation regulations. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also agreed to accept. After convening a meeting of creditors and obtaining their consent, they will try to handle it. The original letter from the company's liquidators to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is as follows: "Dear Sirs, This is to inform you that our Huaying Pharmacy Co., Ltd. was resolved by a special shareholders' meeting on February 28th of this year to cease liquidation, and accountant Xie Lin was elected as the company's liquidator. Later, accountant Xie resigned due to matters, and the company's special shareholders' meeting on June 25th of this year elected our lawyers, accountants, etc., as the company's liquidators. We have taken office and reported to the Shanghai First District Local Court for record. The company's book assets and liabilities were originally offset, but the company's property is mainly composed of medicines and Western medicine raw materials, accounting for about 60% of the total assets. Previously, the book value was advertised for bidding, but no one has inquired about it. If the price is reduced for bidding again, the company's assets will obviously be insufficient to pay off the debts. It is the duty of our lawyers to suspend the liquidation and apply to the court for bankruptcy according to law. However, the value of the pharmaceutical raw materials stored by the company is very large. At this time of commercial failure, a wholesale auction will not only fear that there will be no one to undertake it, but it will also be more difficult to sell it at a good price. Moreover, the legal procedure for applying to the court for bankruptcy will take a long time, and the loss of creditors will be even more unimaginable. After repeated consideration, the lawyers prepared a more favorable mediation plan for the creditors, and in accordance with the new bankruptcy law's mediation regulations, we have attached a statement of property conditions and a list of creditors and debtors, and sent them to your association for inspection, to schedule a meeting of creditors, and to conduct mediation. We sincerely appreciate your public assistance."
